	ajax.request({url: resolvedURLs['ValidateFlow.do'],	params: {validator: 'SHOPPING'}, success: handleFlowValidationResult, dataType: "json"});

	
	
	function handleFlowValidationResult(response) {
		switch (response.flowValidationResult) {
			case "WARNING":
				errorManager.showWarnings([{message: 'The information you are viewing may be out of date. We recommend you begin your search again.'}]);
				break;
			default:
				break;
		}
	}

	function addAir() {
		formManager.submit({form: 'AirFlightItinerarySelectForm', interstBusiness: {content: interstitialContents.airVerifyPrice}});
	}

	
	function replaceAir() {
		popupManager.showConfirmationInfo({
			title: 'Information',
			text: 'There is a flight already in your shopping cart. Would you like to replace it with the selected option?',
			yesHandler: function() { addAir(); }
		});
	}

	
	function removeAir() {
		popupManager.showConfirmationInfo({
			title: 'Information',
			text: 'You have already added the maximum number of flights to your cart. You will have to remove an option from your cart before new options can be added. Would you like to view your cart?',
			yesHandler: function() { window.location.href = 'ItinerarySummary.do'; }
		});
	}

	
	function newSearchAir() {
		popupManager.showConfirmationInfo({
			title: 'Information',
			text: 'You have already added the maximum allowable number of flights to your cart. Start a new search if you would like to begin again. Would you like to view your cart?',
			yesHandler: function() { window.location.href = 'ItinerarySummary.do'; }
		});
	}

	function handleProceedConfirmed() {
		addAir();
	}

	<script type="text/javascript"><!--
		var maxDaysInAdvance = 330;
		var minDaysToDeparture = convertHoursToDays(2);
		Constants = {};
		Constants.dateEntryPattern = "MM/dd/yyyy"; 
		
		function switchModifySearchBlock(lnk) { 
			lnk.blur();
			var stateDiv = lnk.parentNode;
			while (stateDiv.className.indexOf("state") < 0) {
				stateDiv = stateDiv.parentNode;
			}
			if (stateDiv.className.match("Collapsed")) {
				stateDiv.className = stateDiv.className.replace("Collapsed","Expanded");
			} 
			else {
				stateDiv.className = stateDiv.className.replace("Expanded","Collapsed");
			}
		}
	//--></script>
	
	<script type="text/JavaScript"><!--
	    function processModifiedSearchValidationResponse(response, config)
		{
			var form = document.forms['ModifiedFlightSearchForm'];
			errorManager.resetValidationErrors(form);
	
			if (response.status!="success") {
				errorManager.showValidationErrors(response.validationErrors, {form: form});
			}
			else {
				if (form['shopType'])
				{
					switch (previousSelectedTripType)
					{
						case 'RT':
						case 'OW':
							form['shopType'].value = 'SCHEDULE';
							break;
						case 'MC':
							var legCount = 0;
							for (var i = 0; i < 5; i++)
							{
								if (form['multiCityOptions[' + i + '].originLocationName'].value != '')
								{
									legCount++;
								}
							}
							form['shopType'].value = (legCount < 3) ? 'SCHEDULE' : 'PRICE';
							break;
					}
				}
				form.submit();
			}
		}
	
		function processModifiedSearchValidationResponseError(response, config)
		{
			var form = document.forms['ModifiedFlightSearchForm'];
			errorManager.resetValidationErrors(form);
			formManager.error(response, config);
		}
	--></script>

function onBodyLoadAdditional()
{
	dynamicBotComponent.init({context:"airSelection"});

    var selectForm = document.forms['AirFlightItinerarySelectForm'];

    var hiddenSelection = selectForm.elements['hiddenFlightSelection'].value;
    if (hiddenSelection != null && hiddenSelection != "NOT_INITIALIZED")
    {
        var legFlightItineraryArray = hiddenSelection.split(",");
        hiddenFlightSelection = new Array();
        for (var i = 0; i < legFlightItineraryArray.length; i++)
        {
            hiddenFlightSelection[i/2] = [legFlightItineraryArray[i], legFlightItineraryArray[i+1]];
            i++;
        }
    }
    else
    {
        hiddenFlightSelection = new Array();
    }

    if (hiddenFlightSelection != null && hiddenFlightSelection.length > 0)
    {
    	// back button case
    	// do nothing when functionality to reload the full page is enabled
    	if (document.getElementById("pageState_timestamp") == null)
    	{
	        if (activeDates != null && activeDates.length > 0)
	        {
	            ajax.request({
	                url: resolvedURLs['AirReloadOWCFFCalendarSearchResult.do'],
	                params: {
	                    'activeDates' : activeDates,
	                    'isFareFamilySearchResult' : true},
	                success : reloadCalendarResponse,
	                dataType: "json",
	                interstConfig: {}});
	        }
	        else
	        {
	            selectedFlights = new Array();
	            for (var i = 0; i < hiddenFlightSelection.length; i++)
	            {
	                var leg = hiddenFlightSelection[i][0];
	                var flightItineraryId = hiddenFlightSelection[i][1];
	                selectedFlights[i] = [leg, flightItineraryId];

	                var selObj = document.getElementById("flightSelectGr_" + leg + "_" + flightItineraryId);
	                if (selObj)
	                {
	                    fareFamiliesFlightSelection.selectFlight(selObj);
	                }

	                for (var j = 0; j < odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies.length; j++)
	                {
	                    if (odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j] != null
	                            && odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j].length > 0)
	                    {
	                        if (odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][0] == leg
	                            && odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][1] == flightItineraryId)
	                        {
	                            selectFareFamily(leg, odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][2], odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][3]);
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }

	            var selectedFlightIds = "";
	            for (var i = 0; i < selectedFlights.length; i++)
	            {
	                if (selectedFlightIds != "") selectedFlightIds += ",";
	                selectedFlightIds += (selectedFlights[i][0] + "," + selectedFlights[i][1]);
	            }

	            var ajaxConfig =
	            {
	                url: resolvedURLs['AirSelectOWCFlight.do'],
	                success: reloadItinerarySummaryBlock,
	                error: processAjaxRequestError,
	                params: {
	                    'isFareFamilySearchResult' : true,
	                    'selectedItineraries': selectedFlights,
	                    'selectedFlightIds': selectedFlightIds,
	                    'combinabilityReloadRequired' : true,
	                    'flightIndex' : ''
	                }
	            }
	            dynamicBotComponent.update({ajaxConfig: ajaxConfig});
	        }
    	}
    }
    else
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < selectedFlights.length; i++)
        {
            var selObj = document.getElementById("flightSelectGr_" + selectedFlights[i][0] + "_" + selectedFlights[i][1]);
            if (selObj)
            {
                fareFamiliesFlightSelection.selectFlight(selObj);
            }
        }

        
            reloadFlightCombinablility([3]);
        

        nextButtonManagement(2, "");
    }
    fareFamiliesCombinableSearchResultPageView.correctHeight();
    interstitialFramework.hide({});
}

function onClickButtonNext() {
	populateFlightSelection(2);
	checkReservationStatus();
	return false;
}

function onClickViewFareRulesLink(url, flightItineraryId, isReserved) {
	checkFareRulesReservationStatus(url, 2, flightItineraryId, isReserved);
	return false;
}

function reloadItinerarySummaryInfo(o) {
    var selectedLeg = parseInt(o.name.match(/\d+/g));
    var selectedItinerary = parseInt(o.value.match(/\d+/g));

    var selectedFlightsUpdated = false;
    for (var i = 0; i < selectedFlights.length; i++)
    {
        if (selectedFlights[i][0] == selectedLeg)
        {
            selectedFlights[i][1] = selectedItinerary;
            selectedFlightsUpdated = true;
            break;
        }
    }
    if (!selectedFlightsUpdated)
    {
        //selectedFlights[selectedFlights.length] = [selectedLeg, selectedItinerary];
        selectedFlights.splice(selectedLeg, 0, [selectedLeg, selectedItinerary]);
    }

    var selectedFlightIds = "";
    for (var i = 0; i < selectedFlights.length; i++)
    {
        if (selectedFlightIds != "") selectedFlightIds += ",";
        selectedFlightIds += (selectedFlights[i][0] + "," + selectedFlights[i][1]);
    }

    var ajaxConfig =
    {
        url: resolvedURLs['AirSelectOWCFlight.do'],
        success: reloadItinerarySummaryBlock,
        error: processAjaxRequestError,
        params: {
            'isFareFamilySearchResult' : true,
            'selectedItineraries': selectedFlights,
            'selectedFlightIds': selectedFlightIds,
            'combinabilityReloadRequired' : true,
            'flightIndex' : '',
            'flowStep' : "AIR_COMBINABLE_FARE_FAMILIES_SEARCH_RESULTS"
        }
    }

    errorManager.hideWarningBlock();
    dynamicBotComponent.update({ajaxConfig: ajaxConfig});
}

function reloadItinerarySummaryBlock(response, config)
{
	if (response
		&& ((response.topBot && (response.topBot.indexOf("bodySection emptySection") < 0 || response.notFullSelection))
			|| (response.bottomBot && (response.bottomBot.indexOf("bodySection emptySection") < 0 || response.notFullSelection))
			|| (response.sideBot && (response.sideBot.indexOf("bodySection emptySection") < 0) || response.notFullSelection))
		)
    {
        
	            if (document.getElementById('airSelection_SummaryBot_Top') && response.topBot)
	            {
	                document.getElementById('airSelection_SummaryBot_Top').innerHTML = response.topBot;
	            }
                if (document.getElementById('airSelection_SummaryBot_Bottom') && response.bottomBot)
                {
                    document.getElementById('airSelection_SummaryBot_Bottom').innerHTML = response.bottomBot;
                }
            
    }
    else
    {
        
        errorManager.showWarnings([{message: 'We are sorry, we can\'t proceed with this selection. Please reselect.'}]);
    }

	if (response && response.warnings) {
		errorManager.showWarnings(response.warnings);
	}

    
        reloadFlightCombinablility(response.CombinableIds);
    

    if (response && response.notFullSelection) enableNextButton(false);
    else enableNextButton(true);
}

function reloadCalendarResponse(response, config)
{
    if (response.reloadContentData)
    {
        reloadLFSResult(response.contentData);
    }

    selectedFlights = new Array();
    for (var i = 0; i < hiddenFlightSelection.length; i++)
    {
        var leg = hiddenFlightSelection[i][0];
        var flightItineraryId = hiddenFlightSelection[i][1];
        selectedFlights[i] = [leg, flightItineraryId];

        var selObj = document.getElementById("flightSelectGr_" + leg + "_" + flightItineraryId);
        if (selObj)
        {
            fareFamiliesFlightSelection.selectFlight(selObj);
        }

        for (var j = 0; j < odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies.length; j++)
        {
            if (odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j] != null
                    && odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j].length > 0)
            {
                if (odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][0] == leg
                    && odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][1] == flightItineraryId)
                {
                    selectFareFamily(leg, odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][2], odGroupFlightItineraryIdRowsFareFamilies[j][3]);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    var selectedFlightIds = "";
    for (var i = 0; i < selectedFlights.length; i++)
    {
        if (selectedFlightIds != "") selectedFlightIds += ",";
        selectedFlightIds += (selectedFlights[i][0] + "," + selectedFlights[i][1]);
    }

    var ajaxConfig =
    {
        url: resolvedURLs['AirSelectOWCFlight.do'],
        success: reloadItinerarySummaryBlock,
        error: processAjaxRequestError,
        params: {
            'isFareFamilySearchResult' : true,
            'selectedItineraries': selectedFlights,
            'selectedFlightIds': selectedFlightIds,
            'combinabilityReloadRequired' : true,
            'flightIndex' : ''
        }
    }
    errorManager.hideWarningBlock();
    dynamicBotComponent.update({ajaxConfig: ajaxConfig});
}

function reloadFlightCombinablility(combinableItineraries)
{
	if (combinableItineraries === undefined)
	{
		return;
	}
	// Unfortunately we have to cache latest combinable itineraries to restore disabled radio buttons after sorting.
	// TODO [rtorapau]: Think how to avoid it.
	fareFamiliesFlightSelection.cacheCombinableItineraries(combinableItineraries);
    if (selectedFlights.length == 0)
    {
        return;
    }

    var checkedLeg = (selectedFlights[0][0] == 0) ? 1 : 0;

    var checkedFlightItineraries = document.forms["AirFlightItinerarySelectForm"].elements["flightItineraryId[" + checkedLeg + "]"];
    // i.e. we have only 1 returned itinerary
    if (checkedFlightItineraries && checkedFlightItineraries.form)
    {
    	fareFamiliesFlightSelection.checkItinerary(combinableItineraries, checkedFlightItineraries, checkedLeg);
    }
    // i.e. we have an array of itineraries
    else if (checkedFlightItineraries && checkedFlightItineraries.length)
    {
        for (i = 0; i < checkedFlightItineraries.length; i++)
        {
        	fareFamiliesFlightSelection.checkItinerary(combinableItineraries, checkedFlightItineraries[i], checkedLeg);
        }
    }
    var deselectRequired = true;
    if (selectedFlights[1])
    {
        for (i = 0; i < combinableItineraries.length; i++)
        {
            if (selectedFlights[1][1] == combinableItineraries[i])
            {
                deselectRequired = false;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (deselectRequired)
        {
            selectedFlights.length = 1;
        }
    }
}

		function validateForm() {
			var x=document.forms["myForm"]["email"].value;
			var atpos=x.indexOf("@");
			var dotpos=x.lastIndexOf(".");
			if (atpos<1 || dotpos<atpos+2 || dotpos+2>=x.length) {
				alert("Please provide a valid e-mail address");
				return false;
			}
		}
